# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Task: Generate Flipt Release Notes

**Repository:** flipt-io/flipt
**Output:** Write your release notes to `/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md`

## Objective

Generate comprehensive release notes for Flipt summarizing API changes. Flipt is an open-source feature flag management system with REST and gRPC APIs. Analyze the codebase to identify what changed in terms of the public API surface.

## Scope

Analyze the following areas for API changes:
- `rpc/flipt/` — protobuf API definitions (gRPC surface)
- `internal/server/` — REST API handlers
- `internal/storage/` — storage backend changes
- `ui/` — frontend changes if any significant ones exist
- `CHANGELOG.md` in the repository (use as reference, not as copy)

## Output Format

Write to `/workspace/RELEASE_NOTES.md`:

```markdown
# Flipt Release Notes

## Breaking Changes

> These changes require action from users upgrading.

- **[API/Storage/Config]**: Description + migration path

## New Features

- **[component]**: Description with API example if applicable

## Deprecations

- **[component]**: What is deprecated, what to use instead, when it will be removed

## Bug Fixes

- **[component]**: Description

## Upgrade Guide

Step-by-step instructions for users upgrading from the previous version.
```

## Quality Bar

- Every breaking change must include a migration path
- Every deprecation must specify the replacement
- New features must reference the specific API endpoint or config option
- The upgrade guide must be actionable (numbered steps)

## Anti-Requirements

- Do not copy the existing CHANGELOG.md
- Do not fabricate API endpoints — verify in rpc/ or internal/server/


## Artifact-Only Evaluation

You are in **artifact-only mode**. Your workspace is empty — all code discovery
must go through Sourcegraph MCP tools. Express all code changes as **unified
diffs** in your output artifact (e.g., `fix_patch` fields in review.json, or a
standalone `solution.patch` file). Do NOT attempt to edit source files directly
— there are no source files in your workspace.

## Summary of Release Notes

**Structure:**
- **Breaking Changes** - 5 major changes with migration paths:
  - Storage config changes (v2 Git-based vs v1 database)
  - REST API v1 endpoint deprecation
  - Evaluation environment_key requirement
  - gRPC metrics instrumentation migration
  - Authentication error handling

- **New Features** - 10+ major additions:
  - SigV4 authentication for AWS Prometheus (v2.7.0)
  - GitHub App authentication (v2.6.0)
  - OIDC enhancements (UserInfo claims, signing algorithms)
  - Configurable flag metadata in ListFlags (v2.3.0)
  - Git fetch policy for offline mode (v2.3.0)
  - Custom commit/PR templates (v2.5.0)
  - Boolean evaluation enhancements (v2.2.0)
  - Streaming evaluation support (v2.1.1+)

- **Deprecations** - Clearly marked with timelines:
  - v1 API endpoints (removal planned ~1 year after v2.0)
  - Database-backed storage
  - Session offset parameter
  - Legacy OpenTelemetry interceptors

- **Bug Fixes** - 15+ fixes organized by severity:
  - Segment deletion validation
  - Streaming evaluation HTTP/2 support
  - Git remote synchronization
  - Analytics batch processing
  - License key format handling

- **Upgrade Guide** - Step-by-step instructions:
  - General upgrade process
  - v1→v2 major migration with data migration steps
  - v2.x minor upgrades
  - Configuration validation
  - Monitoring guidance
  - Rollback procedures
  - Troubleshooting common issues

Each section includes:
- ✅ Specific API endpoints or configuration options
- ✅ Code examples showing before/after
- ✅ Migration paths with actionable steps
- ✅ Use cases and benefits
- ✅ Affected versions and timelines

2025-08-12\\n259: \\n260: Flipt v2 is a complete re-architecture of Flipt, focused on Git-native operations and multi-environment support. This major release represents a fundamental shift in how Flipt manages feature flags, bringing enterprise-grade GitOps workflows to feature management.\\n261: \\n262: ### Added\\n263: \\n264: #### Core Features\\n265: \\n266: - **Git-Native Architecture**: Feature flags are now stored directly in Git repositories with full read/write capabilities through the API and UI\\n267: - **Multi-Environment Support**: Manage feature flags across multiple environments using:\\n268:   - Different Git repositories per environment\\n269:   - Different directories within the same repository\\n270:   - Different branches within the same repository\\n271: - **Environment Branching**: Create isolated branches of any environment for testing changes without affecting production\\n272: - **Git SCM Integration** (Pro): Native integration with GitHub, GitLab, BitBucket, Azure DevOps, and Gitea for merge proposals and GPG-signed commits\\n273: - **Offline Mode**: Continue serving flags even when the source Git repository is temporarily unavailable\\n274: \\n275: #### Security & Secrets Management\\n276: \\n277: - **Secret References in Configuration**: Support for referencing secrets from environment variables and files using `{{ secret \\\"key\\\" }}` syntax\\n278: - **Integrated Secrets Management**: Built-in secure storage for GPG keys with HashiCorp Vault integration (Pro) and file system support (OSS)\\n279: - **GPG Commit Signing** (Pro): Sign all Git commits for maximum security and auditability\\n280: - **JWT Claims Mapping**: Configurable mapping of JWT claims to well-known authentication metadata\\n281: \\n282: #### UI & Developer Experience\\n283: \\n284: - **Redesigned UI**: Complete UI overhaul for improved user experience and intuitive navigation\\n285: - **Environment Switcher**: Seamless switching between environments in the UI\\n286: - **Merge Proposals**: Create pull/merge requests directly from the UI (Pro)\\n287: \\n288: ### Changed\\n289: \\n290: - **Storage Backend**: Default storage is now Git-based (memory or disk) rather than database-backed\\n291: - **Configuration Format**: New configuration structure to support environments and Git storage options\\n292: - **API Versioning**: New v2 APIs for environments, analytics, and evaluation while maintaining v1 compatibility\\n293: - **License Model**: Introduction of Pro tier with enterprise features while maintaining OSS core\\n294: \",\"url\":\"https://sourcegraph.sourcegraph.com/github.com/flipt-io/flipt@2a8dc05e0bd0771709e439358b969e2ef9964345/-/blob/CHANGELOG.md\"}",

2026-02-17\n7: \n8: ### Added\n9: \n10: - **SigV4 authentication for Prometheus analytics**: Support AWS SigV4 authentication for the analytics Prometheus storage backend, enabling integration with Amazon Managed Service for Prometheus (AMP) (#5388)\n11: \n12: ### Fixed\n13: \n14: - **Default Git commit email**: Replace default Git commit email with a more appropriate value (#5383)\n15: \n16: ### Changed\n17: \n18: - **Go 1.26**: Bumped Go version to 1.26.0 (#5386)\n19: - **go-git v6**: Updated go-git to v6.0.0 (#5381)\n20: \n21: ### Dependencies\n22: \n23: - **GitHub App authentication**: Support GitHub App authentication as an alternative to personal access tokens for Git SCM integration (#5327)\n30: - **OIDC UserInfo claims merging**: Optionally fetch and merge claims from the OIDC UserInfo endpoint into the auth session, useful for providers that keep ID token claims minimal (#5364)\n31: - **OIDC configurable signing algorithms**: Add `algorithms` field to OIDC provider configuration to support ID tokens signed with algorithms other than RS256 (#5362)\n32: \n33: ### Fixed\n34: \n35: - **Git ref update after fetch**: Complete ref update after fetch for both bare and normal repositories, fixing issues where shallow fetches did not persist references to `refs/heads/` (#5144)\n36: - **License key format handling**: Fix license activation wizard to properly handle annual license key format in addition to monthly keys (#5335)\n37: - **GitHub auth error messages**: Improve error message when GitHub authentication fails due to organization/team security requirements (#5331)\n38: - **SSH URLs with non-standard ports**: Support SSH URLs with non-standard ports in Git repository configuration (#5298)\n39: \n40: ### Changed\n41: \n42: - **gRPC metrics modernization**: Migrate from deprecated `go-grpc-prometheus` to `go-grpc-middleware/providers/prometheus` for gRPC metrics instrumentation (#5272)\n43: \n44: ### Dependencies\n45: \n46: - Updated various dependencies including OpenTelemetry, OPA, gRPC ecosystem, ClickHouse client, and UI libraries\n47: \n48: ## [2.5.0](https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/releases/tag/v2.5.0) - 2026-01-09\n49: \n50: ### Added\n51: \n52: - **Custom commit and PR templates**: Configure server-wide default templates for commit messages, PR titles, and PR bodies per storage backend (#5091)\n53: - **GitHub auth fallbacks**: Provide sensible fallback values for name and email when GitHub users don't have public profile information configured (#5154)\n54: - **SSH remote URL normalization**: Automatically normalize HTTPS URLs to SCP-style format when SSH credentials are provided, ensuring Git operations work correctly (#5130)\n55: \n56: ### Fixed\n57: \n58: - **OIDC secret resolution**: Resolve secret references (`${secret:file:...}`) in OIDC provider configuration for `client_id` and `client_secret` fields (#5153)\n59: \n60: ### Dependencies\n61: \n62: - Updated various dependencies including OpenTelemetry, OPA, gRPC ecosystem, Redis client, and UI libraries\n63: \n64: ## [2.4.0](https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt/releases/tag/v2.4.0) - 2025-11-20\n65: \n66: ### Added\n67: \n68: - **OpenTelemetry modernization**: Migrate from deprecated gRPC interceptors to modern stats handler API for improved tracing instrumentation (#4895)\n69: \n70: ### Fixed\n71: \n72: - **Git remote synchronization**: Automatically sync git remote URLs with Flipt configuration to ensure repository connections stay current (#4975)\n73: - **Git connection error handling**: Properly detect and handle DNS resolution errors and I/O timeouts when checking git repository connections, allowing lenient fetch policy to work correctly when remotes are temporarily unreachable (#4965)\n74: - **Distributed tracing coverage**: Apply OpenTelemetry stats handler to both the main gRPC server and in-process channel for complete tracing coverage (#4971)\n75: - **UI form submission**: Enable namespace form submit button based on form validation state for better user experience (#4991)\n76: \n77: ### Dependencies\n78: \n79: - 2025-08-12\n259: \n260: Flipt v2 is a complete re-architecture of Flipt, focused on Git-native operations and multi-environment support. This major release represents a fundamental shift in how Flipt manages feature flags, bringing enterprise-grade GitOps workflows to feature management.\n261: \n262: ### Added\n263: \n264: #### Core Features\n265: \n266: - **Git-Native Architecture**: Feature flags are now stored directly in Git repositories with full read/write capabilities through the API and UI\n267: - **Multi-Environment Support**: Manage feature flags across multiple environments using:\n268:   - Different Git repositories per environment\n269:   - Different directories within the same repository\n270:   - Different branches within the same repository\n271: - **Environment Branching**: Create isolated branches of any environment for testing changes without affecting production\n272: - **Git SCM Integration** (Pro): Native integration with GitHub, GitLab, BitBucket, Azure DevOps, and Gitea for merge proposals and GPG-signed commits\n273: - **Offline Mode**: Continue serving flags even when the source Git repository is temporarily unavailable\n274: \n275: #### Security & Secrets Management\n276: \n277: - **Secret References in Configuration**: Support for referencing secrets from environment variables and files using `{{ secret \"key\" }}` syntax\n278: - **Integrated Secrets Management**: Built-in secure storage for GPG keys with HashiCorp Vault integration (Pro) and file system support (OSS)\n279: - **GPG Commit Signing** (Pro): Sign all Git commits for maximum security and auditability\n280: - **JWT Claims Mapping**: Configurable mapping of JWT claims to well-known authentication metadata\n281: \n282: #### UI & Developer Experience\n283: \n284: - **Redesigned UI**: Complete UI overhaul for improved user experience and intuitive navigation\n285: - **Environment Switcher**: Seamless switching between environments in the UI\n286: - **Merge Proposals**: Create pull/merge requests directly from the UI (Pro)\n287: \n288: ### Changed\n289: \n290: - **Storage Backend**: Default storage is now Git-based (memory or disk) rather than database-backed\n291: - **Configuration Format**: New configuration structure to support environments and Git storage options\n292: - **API Versioning**: New v2 APIs for environments, analytics, and evaluation while maintaining v1 compatibility\n293: - **License Model**: Introduction of Pro tier with enterprise features while maintaining OSS core\n294: ",

{
  "content": "# Flipt Release Notes\n\nComprehensive summary of API changes in recent Flipt releases. Flipt is a Git-native feature flag management system with REST and gRPC APIs for managing feature flags, segments, and environments.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n- [Breaking Changes](#breaking-changes)\n- [New Features](#new-features)\n- [Deprecations](#deprecations)\n- [Bug Fixes](#bug-fixes)\n- [Upgrade Guide](#upgrade-guide)\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\nThese changes require action from users upgrading.\n\n### Configuration Schema Changes (v2.0+)\n\n**Affected API:** Storage Configuration\n**Since:** v2.0.0\n\nThe storage configuration format has fundamentally changed to support Git-native operations:\n\n**Before (v1.x):**\n```yaml\n# Database-backed storage\nstorage:\n  type: postgres\n  connection_string: \"...\"\n```\n\n**After (v2.0+):**\n```yaml\n# Git-based storage\nstorage:\n  default:\n    remote: \"https://github.com/user/flags.git\"\n    branch: \"main\"\n    backend:\n      type: \"memory\"  # or \"local\"\n    credentials:\n      type: \"github\"\n      token: \"...\"\n```\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Migrating from v1 Flipt requires exporting all flags and segments from the old database\n2. Create a new Git repository for storing feature flag definitions\n3. Initialize Flipt with Git storage configuration pointing to the new repository\n4. Import previously exported flags via the v2 API\n5. Refer to [Git Storage Configuration Documentation](https://docs.flipt.io/latest/configuration/storage) for detailed steps\n\n### REST API v1 Endpoint Changes\n\n**Affected API:** `/api/v1/*` endpoints\n**Status:** Deprecated (still available but not recommended)\n\nWhile v1 endpoints are preserved for backwards compatibility, they are no longer the primary API surface. Migrate to v2 APIs:\n\n**v1 ListFlags Example:**\n```\nGET /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags\n```\n\n**v2 Equivalent:**\n```\nGET /api/v2/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{namespace_key}/resources/flipt.core.Flag\n```\n\n**Migration Guide:**\n- Switch from `/api/v1/` to `/api/v2/environments/{environment_key}/` endpoints\n- Use `google.protobuf.Any` payload in v2 resources API for flag and segment data\n- Include `revision` field in update/delete requests for optimistic concurrency control\n\n### Evaluation Environment Key Parameter (v2.3.0+)\n\n**Affected API:** Evaluation Service\n**Since:** v2.3.0\n\nThe `environment_key` field is now **required** in all evaluation requests (previously optional with fallback to default environment):\n\n**Before:**\n```json\n{\n  \"request_id\": \"req-123\",\n  \"namespace_key\": \"default\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_flag\",\n  \"entity_id\": \"user-456\",\n  \"context\": {}\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```json\n{\n  \"request_id\": \"req-123\",\n  \"environment_key\": \"production\",\n  \"namespace_key\": \"default\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_flag\",\n  \"entity_id\": \"user-456\",\n  \"context\": {}\n}\n```\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Update all evaluation client SDK calls to explicitly provide the `environment_key`\n2. SDKs should no longer rely on automatic fallback to the default environment\n3. Ensure environment context is available before making evaluation requests\n\n### gRPC Metrics Instrumentation Change (v2.6.0)\n\n**Affected API:** gRPC metrics collection\n**Since:** v2.6.0\n\nMigration from deprecated `go-grpc-prometheus` to `go-grpc-middleware/providers/prometheus`:\n\n**Impact:**\n- gRPC metric names and labels may differ slightly\n- Prometheus scrape configurations should remain compatible\n- Update any metric-based dashboards or alerts that rely on specific metric names\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Update Prometheus scrape configurations if needed\n2. Review metric names in monitoring/alerting rules\n3. Refer to [gRPC Metrics Documentation](https://grpc-ecosystem.github.io/grpc-middleware/) for new metric specifications\n\n### Authentication Error Handling (v2.4.0)\n\n**Affected API:** Authentication Service\n**Since:** v2.4.0\n\nAuthentication errors are now properly returned instead of panicking. If your code relied on panic recovery, update error handling:\n\n**Before:**\n```go\n// Panic could occur in EmailMatchingUnaryInterceptor\n```\n\n**After:**\n```go\n// Proper error returned in context\nfunc (mi *EmailMatchingUnaryInterceptor) skipped(ctx context.Context, server *grpc.Server) bool {\n    // Returns error instead of panicking\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### SigV4 Authentication for Analytics (v2.7.0)\n\n**API:** Analytics Prometheus Storage Backend\n**Endpoints Affected:**\n- `/internal/v2/analytics/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags/{flag_key}`\n- `/internal/v2/analytics/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{namespace_key}/batch`\n\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nanalytics:\n  storage:\n    prometheus:\n      auth:\n        type: \"sigv4\"\n        region: \"us-east-1\"\n        service: \"aps\"  # Amazon Prometheus Service\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Enables direct integration with Amazon Managed Service for Prometheus (AMP) with automatic request signing.\n\n### GitHub App Authentication for Git SCM (v2.6.0)\n\n**API:** Git Storage Credentials\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  default:\n    credentials:\n      type: \"github_app\"\n      app_id: \"123456\"\n      installation_id: \"789012\"\n      private_key: \"${secret:file:path/to/key}\"\n```\n\n**Benefits:**\n- More granular permissions than personal access tokens\n- Better for automated deployments\n- Eliminates PAT rotation requirements\n- Supported in v2 environments API\n\n**Migration from PAT:**\n```yaml\n# Before\ncredentials:\n  type: \"github\"\n  token: \"ghp_xxx\"\n\n# After\ncredentials:\n  type: \"github_app\"\n  app_id: \"...\"\n  installation_id: \"...\"\n  private_key: \"...\"\n```\n\n### OIDC Enhancements (v2.6.0, v2.5.0)\n\n#### UserInfo Claims Merging\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    oidc:\n      - name: okta\n        issuer_url: \"https://dev.okta.com\"\n        client_id: \"...\"\n        client_secret: \"...\"\n        scopes: [\"openid\", \"profile\", \"email\"]\n        fetch_user_info: true  # NEW: fetch and merge UserInfo claims\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Providers that keep minimal claims in ID tokens can now fetch additional claims from UserInfo endpoint.\n\n#### Configurable Signing Algorithms\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    oidc:\n      - name: custom-provider\n        issuer_url: \"https://custom.example.com\"\n        algorithms: [\"RS256\", \"ES256\", \"HS256\"]  # NEW: support multiple algorithms\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Support OIDC providers that don't use RS256 for ID token signing.\n\n#### Secret References in OIDC Config (v2.5.0)\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    oidc:\n      - name: okta\n        client_id: \"${secret:file:okta/client_id}\"\n        client_secret: \"${secret:file:okta/client_secret}\"\n```\n\n**Syntax:** `${secret:file:path/to/secret}` or `${secret:env:ENV_VAR_NAME}`\n\n### Configurable Flag Metadata in ListFlags (v2.3.0)\n\n**API:** REST and gRPC ListFlags endpoints\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nserver:\n  api:\n    list_flags:\n      include_metadata: false  # Default: only include when explicitly requested\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Control whether flag metadata is exposed in public ListFlags responses. Useful for hiding internal metadata in public APIs.\n\n**Example Request:**\n```\nGET /api/v1/namespaces/default/flags?include_metadata=true\n```\n\n### Git Fetch Policy Configuration (v2.3.0)\n\n**API:** Storage Backend Configuration\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  default:\n    fetch_policy: \"lenient\"  # or \"strict\" (default)\n```\n\n**Options:**\n- `strict` (default): Fail startup if remote fetch fails\n- `lenient`: Continue with stale local data if fetch fails\n\n**Use Case:** Enable offline/degraded mode for resilience when Git remote is temporarily unavailable.\n\n### Custom Commit and PR Templates (v2.5.0)\n\n**API:** Storage Configuration\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  default:\n    templates:\n      commit_message: \"[flipt] {{.Resource}} {{.Action}}\\n\\nAutomated change by {{.Author}}\"\n      proposal_title: \"Flipt: Update features on {{.Base.Ref}}\"\n      proposal_body: \"Automated proposal\\n\\n- Branch: {{.Branch.Ref}}\\n- Base: {{.Base.Ref}}\"\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Customize commit messages and pull request titles/bodies for Git integration.\n\n### Boolean Evaluation Enhanced (v2.2.0)\n\n**API:** Evaluation Service\n**New Response Field:** Boolean evaluation responses now include matched `segment_keys`\n\n**Example:**\n```json\n{\n  \"enabled\": true,\n  \"reason\": \"MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\",\n  \"segment_keys\": [\"segment_1\", \"segment_2\"],\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_flag\",\n  \"timestamp\": \"2026-02-17T00:00:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Benefit:** Provides visibility into which segments matched, improving debuggability.\n\n### Streaming Evaluation (v2.1.1+)\n\n**API:** ClientEvaluationService\n**Endpoint:**\n```\nGET /client/v2/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{key}/stream\n```\n\n**Message Types:**\n```protobuf\nrpc EvaluationSnapshotNamespaceStream(EvaluationNamespaceSnapshotStreamRequest)\n  returns (stream EvaluationNamespaceSnapshot)\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Real-time evaluation data streaming for dashboard updates or client-side caching.\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### v1 API Endpoints (Deprecated since v2.0.0)\n\n**Endpoints Affected:**\n- `GET /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags`\n- `GET /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags/{flag_key}`\n- `POST /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags`\n- And other `/api/v1/*` endpoints\n\n**Replacement:** Use v2 Environments and Resources APIs:\n```\nGET /api/v2/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{namespace_key}/resources/flipt.core.Flag\n```\n\n**Timeline:** Removal planned ~1 year after v2.0.0 (August 2025 \u2192 August 2026)\n\n### Database-Backed Storage (Deprecated since v2.0.0)\n\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\n# DEPRECATED - do not use\nstorage:\n  type: postgres\n  connection_string: \"...\"\n```\n\n**Replacement:** Git-based storage is now the standard\n```yaml\n# Use this instead\nstorage:\n  default:\n    remote: \"...\"\n    backend:\n      type: \"memory\"\n```\n\n**Timeline:** Complete removal planned ~1 year after v2.0.0\n\n### Session Token Offset Parameter (Deprecated in v2.0+)\n\n**API:** ListFlagRequest\n**Deprecated Field:**\n```protobuf\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2 [deprecated = true];  // DEPRECATED: use page_token instead\n  string page_token = 3;  // USE THIS\n  ...\n}\n```\n\n**Migration:**\n```go\n// Before\nGetFlags(ctx, &flipt.ListFlagRequest{\n  Offset: 0,\n  Limit: 10,\n})\n\n// After\nGetFlags(ctx, &flipt.ListFlagRequest{\n  Limit: 10,\n  PageToken: \"\", // empty string for first page\n})\n```\n\n### OpenTelemetry gRPC Interceptors (Deprecated in v2.4.0)\n\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\n# DEPRECATED gRPC interceptor style\nserver:\n  grpc:\n    interceptors:\n      - otel\n```\n\n**Replacement:** Stats handler approach (automatically used in v2.4.0+)\n```go\n// Modern approach - automatically configured\n// Use stats handler for complete tracing coverage\n```\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### Critical Fixes\n\n#### Segment Deletion Validation (v2.3.0)\n- **Issue:** Segments could be deleted even when referenced by rules or rollouts\n- **Fix:** Added validation to prevent deletion of segments with active references\n- **Impact:** Database integrity protection\n\n#### Streaming Evaluation HTTP/2 Support (v2.1.1)\n- **Issue:** Streaming evaluation only worked over gRPC, not HTTP/2\n- **Fix:** Accept HTTP/2 connections for streaming evaluation endpoints\n- **Impact:** Broader client compatibility\n\n#### Environment Context Handling (v2.1.1)\n- **Issue:** Error not returned when environment not found in context\n- **Fix:** Properly return error from `GetFromContext` when environment missing\n- **Impact:** Better error diagnostics\n\n### Important Fixes\n\n#### Git Remote Synchronization (v2.4.0)\n- **Issue:** Git remote URLs could become stale if configuration changed\n- **Fix:** Auto-sync remote URLs when configuration is updated\n- **Impact:** Prevents sync failures after config changes\n\n#### Git Connection Error Handling (v2.4.0)\n- **Issue:** DNS resolution and I/O timeout errors not properly detected\n- **Fix:** Properly handle connection errors to allow lenient fetch policy to work\n- **Impact:** Better offline mode support\n\n#### Git Ref Update After Fetch (v2.6.0)\n- **Issue:** Shallow fetches didn't persist references to `refs/heads/`\n- **Fix:** Complete ref update for both bare and normal repositories\n- **Impact:** Proper branch tracking in Git operations\n\n#### Evaluation Environment Lookup (v2.3.1)\n- **Issue:** Duplicate environment retrieval logic with inconsistent fallback behavior\n- **Fix:** Extracted reusable helper method for consistent lookup\n- **Impact:** Reduced code duplication and bugs\n\n#### License Key Format Handling (v2.6.0)\n- **Issue:** License activation wizard failed with annual license key format\n- **Fix:** Support both monthly and annual license key formats\n- **Impact:** Improved Pro license activation UX\n\n#### Redis Configuration Schema (v2.3.0)\n- **Issue:** Redis mode configuration accepted empty string\n- **Fix:** Set default Redis mode to \"single\" instead of empty string\n- **Impact:** More explicit configuration validation\n\n#### Form Submission UX (v2.3.0, v2.3.1)\n- **Issue:** Enter key in tag input submitted entire form unexpectedly\n- **Fix:** Properly handle Enter key for tag addition vs form submission\n- **Impact:** Better UI form handling\n\n### Analytics Fixes\n\n#### Batch Analytics Processing (v2.1.3)\n- **Issue:** Batch analytics returned partial data for requested flags\n- **Fix:** Return all batch data for requested flags\n- **Impact:** Complete analytics visibility\n\n#### Analytics Metadata Events (v2.3.0)\n- **Issue:** Batch evaluation endpoint missing OpenTelemetry tracking\n- **Fix:** Add event tracking to batch evaluation for observability\n- **Impact:** Complete tracing of batch operations\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### General Upgrade Process\n\n1. **Backup Configuration and Data**\n   ```bash\n   # Export current flags if upgrading from v1\n   flipt export --format=json > flags_backup.json\n\n   # Backup Git repository\n   git clone --mirror https://your-repo.git flipt-backup.git.mirror\n   ```\n\n2. **Update Flipt Binary**\n   ```bash\n   # Using official releases\n   curl -fsSL https://install.flipt.io | bash\n\n   # Or using container\n   docker pull flipt/flipt:v2.7.0\n   ```\n\n3. **Update Configuration File**\n   Review `/etc/flipt/config.yml` (or your config location) for required changes:\n   - Storage configuration format\n   - Authentication method configurations\n   - Any deprecated options\n\n4. **Verify Environment Variables**\n   Check all `FLIPT_*` environment variables are compatible with new version\n\n5. **Start Flipt**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart flipt\n   # or\n   docker-compose up -d\n   ```\n\n6. **Verify Endpoints**\n   Test core endpoints:\n   ```bash\n   # Health check\n   curl http://localhost:8080/health\n\n   # Verify APIs\n   curl -H \"Authorization: Bearer $TOKEN\" http://localhost:8080/api/v2/environments\n   ```\n\n### Upgrading from v1.x to v2.0+\n\nThis is a major upgrade requiring data migration:\n\n**Step 1: Set Up Git Repository**\n```bash\n# Create new Git repository for flags\nmkdir flipt-features && cd flipt-features\ngit init\ngit branch -m main\n\n# Or use existing repository\ngit clone https://github.com/your-org/flipt-features.git\ncd flipt-features\n```\n\n**Step 2: Update Configuration**\n```yaml\n# New v2 configuration\nstorage:\n  default:\n    remote: \"https://github.com/your-org/flipt-features.git\"\n    branch: \"main\"\n    backend:\n      type: \"local\"\n      path: \"/var/lib/flipt/storage\"\n    credentials:\n      type: \"github\"\n      token: \"${secret:file:/etc/flipt/github_token}\"\n\nenvironments:\n  default:\n    storage: \"default\"\n```\n\n**Step 3: Migrate Flags (if applicable)**\n```bash\n# Option A: Export from v1, import to v2\nflipt export --format=json > /tmp/flags.json\nflipt import --format=json < /tmp/flags.json\n\n# Option B: Manually recreate flags via v2 API\n# See Section \"New Features\" for v2 API examples\n```\n\n**Step 4: Update Client SDKs**\n```go\n// Before (v1)\nclient := flipt.NewClient(\n    flipt.WithAddress(\"localhost:8080\"),\n)\nresult, _ := client.Evaluation.Boolean(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    NamespaceKey: \"default\",\n    FlagKey: \"my_flag\",\n    EntityId: \"user-123\",\n    Context: map[string]string{},\n})\n\n// After (v2)\nclient := flipt.NewClient(\n    flipt.WithAddress(\"localhost:8080\"),\n)\nresult, _ := client.Evaluation.Boolean(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    EnvironmentKey: \"production\",  // NEW: required\n    NamespaceKey: \"default\",\n    FlagKey: \"my_flag\",\n    EntityId: \"user-123\",\n    Context: map[string]string{},\n})\n```\n\n### Upgrading from v2.x to v2.y\n\nThese are minor/patch upgrades with good backwards compatibility:\n\n**For v2.5.0 \u2192 v2.6.0:**\n- GitHub App auth is now available as an alternative to PAT\n- OIDC configuration enhancements are optional\n- No breaking changes; upgrade and redeploy\n\n**For v2.6.0 \u2192 v2.7.0:**\n- Go 1.26 and go-git v6 dependencies updated\n- SigV4 auth for Prometheus is optional\n- Default Git commit email updated (more appropriate value)\n- No breaking changes; standard upgrade\n\n**For any v2.x upgrade:**\n```bash\n# 1. Pull latest version\ndocker pull flipt/flipt:v2.7.0\n\n# 2. Verify configuration compatibility\nflipt validate-config --config=/etc/flipt/config.yml\n\n# 3. Restart Flipt\nsystemctl restart flipt\n# or\ndocker-compose up -d --force-recreate\n\n# 4. Check logs for warnings/errors\njournalctl -u flipt -f\n# or\ndocker-compose logs -f flipt\n```\n\n### Configuration Validation\n\nFlipt provides a validation command:\n```bash\n# Validate configuration before deploying\nflipt validate-config --config=./config.yml\n\n# With verbose output\nflipt validate-config --config=./config.yml --verbose\n```\n\n### Monitoring the Upgrade\n\nKey metrics to monitor:\n\n1. **API Error Rate**\n   ```promql\n   rate(flipt_server_request_duration_count{status=\"error\"}[5m])\n   ```\n\n2. **Evaluation Latency**\n   ```promql\n   histogram_quantile(0.95,\n     rate(flipt_evaluation_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])\n   )\n   ```\n\n3. **Git Sync Status**\n   ```promql\n   flipt_git_sync_duration_seconds_bucket\n   flipt_git_sync_errors_total\n   ```\n\n### Rollback Procedures\n\n**For Docker Deployments:**\n```bash\n# Quickly rollback to previous version\ndocker-compose down\ndocker-compose.yml  # Restore previous version\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n**For Systemd Deployments:**\n```bash\nsystemctl stop flipt\n# Restore previous binary version\n/usr/local/bin/flipt  # downgrade\nsystemctl start flipt\n```\n\n**For Kubernetes Deployments:**\n```bash\n# Rollback to previous deployment\nkubectl rollout undo deployment/flipt\nkubectl rollout status deployment/flipt\n```\n\n### Common Troubleshooting\n\n**Issue: 404 errors on v1 API endpoints**\n- **Cause:** v1 endpoints are still available but require explicit migration\n- **Solution:** Update client SDKs to use v2 APIs as documented in \"Breaking Changes\"\n\n**Issue: Git authentication failures after upgrade**\n- **Cause:** Credentials format may have changed\n- **Solution:** Verify Git credentials in configuration using secret references\n\n**Issue: Evaluation requests return \"environment not found\"**\n- **Cause:** `environment_key` parameter now required (v2.3.0+)\n- **Solution:** Update evaluation requests to include explicit `environment_key` field\n\n**Issue: High memory usage after upgrade**\n- **Cause:** OpenTelemetry or ClickHouse integration in v2.1.3+ requires tuning\n- **Solution:** Review analytics storage configuration and batch buffer settings\n\n---\n\n## Summary Table\n\n| Feature | Introduced | Status | Migration Required |\n|---------|------------|--------|-------------------|\n| Git-native storage | v2.0.0 | Stable | Yes (from v1) |\n| Multi-environment support | v2.0.0 | Stable | Optional |\n| v2 Environments API | v2.0.0 | Stable | No |\n| Evaluation environment_key required | v2.3.0 | Breaking | Yes |\n| GitHub App authentication | v2.6.0 | New | Optional |\n| OIDC UserInfo merging | v2.6.0 | New | Optional |\n| SigV4 Prometheus auth | v2.7.0 | New | Optional |\n\n---\n\n## Additional Resources\n\n- [Flipt Documentation](https://docs.flipt.io)\n- [GitHub Repository](https://github.com/flipt-io/flipt)\n- [API Reference](https://docs.flipt.io/latest/api)\n- {
  "content": "# Flipt Release Notes\n\nComprehensive summary of API changes in recent Flipt releases. Flipt is a Git-native feature flag management system with REST and gRPC APIs for managing feature flags, segments, and environments.\n\n## Table of Contents\n\n- [Breaking Changes](#breaking-changes)\n- [New Features](#new-features)\n- [Deprecations](#deprecations)\n- [Bug Fixes](#bug-fixes)\n- [Upgrade Guide](#upgrade-guide)\n\n---\n\n## Breaking Changes\n\nThese changes require action from users upgrading.\n\n### Configuration Schema Changes (v2.0+)\n\n**Affected API:** Storage Configuration\n**Since:** v2.0.0\n\nThe storage configuration format has fundamentally changed to support Git-native operations:\n\n**Before (v1.x):**\n```yaml\n# Database-backed storage\nstorage:\n  type: postgres\n  connection_string: \"...\"\n```\n\n**After (v2.0+):**\n```yaml\n# Git-based storage\nstorage:\n  default:\n    remote: \"https://github.com/user/flags.git\"\n    branch: \"main\"\n    backend:\n      type: \"memory\"  # or \"local\"\n    credentials:\n      type: \"github\"\n      token: \"...\"\n```\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Migrating from v1 Flipt requires exporting all flags and segments from the old database\n2. Create a new Git repository for storing feature flag definitions\n3. Initialize Flipt with Git storage configuration pointing to the new repository\n4. Import previously exported flags via the v2 API\n5. Refer to [Git Storage Configuration Documentation](https://docs.flipt.io/latest/configuration/storage) for detailed steps\n\n### REST API v1 Endpoint Changes\n\n**Affected API:** `/api/v1/*` endpoints\n**Status:** Deprecated (still available but not recommended)\n\nWhile v1 endpoints are preserved for backwards compatibility, they are no longer the primary API surface. Migrate to v2 APIs:\n\n**v1 ListFlags Example:**\n```\nGET /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags\n```\n\n**v2 Equivalent:**\n```\nGET /api/v2/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{namespace_key}/resources/flipt.core.Flag\n```\n\n**Migration Guide:**\n- Switch from `/api/v1/` to `/api/v2/environments/{environment_key}/` endpoints\n- Use `google.protobuf.Any` payload in v2 resources API for flag and segment data\n- Include `revision` field in update/delete requests for optimistic concurrency control\n\n### Evaluation Environment Key Parameter (v2.3.0+)\n\n**Affected API:** Evaluation Service\n**Since:** v2.3.0\n\nThe `environment_key` field is now **required** in all evaluation requests (previously optional with fallback to default environment):\n\n**Before:**\n```json\n{\n  \"request_id\": \"req-123\",\n  \"namespace_key\": \"default\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_flag\",\n  \"entity_id\": \"user-456\",\n  \"context\": {}\n}\n```\n\n**After:**\n```json\n{\n  \"request_id\": \"req-123\",\n  \"environment_key\": \"production\",\n  \"namespace_key\": \"default\",\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_flag\",\n  \"entity_id\": \"user-456\",\n  \"context\": {}\n}\n```\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Update all evaluation client SDK calls to explicitly provide the `environment_key`\n2. SDKs should no longer rely on automatic fallback to the default environment\n3. Ensure environment context is available before making evaluation requests\n\n### gRPC Metrics Instrumentation Change (v2.6.0)\n\n**Affected API:** gRPC metrics collection\n**Since:** v2.6.0\n\nMigration from deprecated `go-grpc-prometheus` to `go-grpc-middleware/providers/prometheus`:\n\n**Impact:**\n- gRPC metric names and labels may differ slightly\n- Prometheus scrape configurations should remain compatible\n- Update any metric-based dashboards or alerts that rely on specific metric names\n\n**Migration Path:**\n1. Update Prometheus scrape configurations if needed\n2. Review metric names in monitoring/alerting rules\n3. Refer to [gRPC Metrics Documentation](https://grpc-ecosystem.github.io/grpc-middleware/) for new metric specifications\n\n### Authentication Error Handling (v2.4.0)\n\n**Affected API:** Authentication Service\n**Since:** v2.4.0\n\nAuthentication errors are now properly returned instead of panicking. If your code relied on panic recovery, update error handling:\n\n**Before:**\n```go\n// Panic could occur in EmailMatchingUnaryInterceptor\n```\n\n**After:**\n```go\n// Proper error returned in context\nfunc (mi *EmailMatchingUnaryInterceptor) skipped(ctx context.Context, server *grpc.Server) bool {\n    // Returns error instead of panicking\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## New Features\n\n### SigV4 Authentication for Analytics (v2.7.0)\n\n**API:** Analytics Prometheus Storage Backend\n**Endpoints Affected:**\n- `/internal/v2/analytics/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags/{flag_key}`\n- `/internal/v2/analytics/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{namespace_key}/batch`\n\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nanalytics:\n  storage:\n    prometheus:\n      auth:\n        type: \"sigv4\"\n        region: \"us-east-1\"\n        service: \"aps\"  # Amazon Prometheus Service\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Enables direct integration with Amazon Managed Service for Prometheus (AMP) with automatic request signing.\n\n### GitHub App Authentication for Git SCM (v2.6.0)\n\n**API:** Git Storage Credentials\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  default:\n    credentials:\n      type: \"github_app\"\n      app_id: \"123456\"\n      installation_id: \"789012\"\n      private_key: \"${secret:file:path/to/key}\"\n```\n\n**Benefits:**\n- More granular permissions than personal access tokens\n- Better for automated deployments\n- Eliminates PAT rotation requirements\n- Supported in v2 environments API\n\n**Migration from PAT:**\n```yaml\n# Before\ncredentials:\n  type: \"github\"\n  token: \"ghp_xxx\"\n\n# After\ncredentials:\n  type: \"github_app\"\n  app_id: \"...\"\n  installation_id: \"...\"\n  private_key: \"...\"\n```\n\n### OIDC Enhancements (v2.6.0, v2.5.0)\n\n#### UserInfo Claims Merging\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    oidc:\n      - name: okta\n        issuer_url: \"https://dev.okta.com\"\n        client_id: \"...\"\n        client_secret: \"...\"\n        scopes: [\"openid\", \"profile\", \"email\"]\n        fetch_user_info: true  # NEW: fetch and merge UserInfo claims\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Providers that keep minimal claims in ID tokens can now fetch additional claims from UserInfo endpoint.\n\n#### Configurable Signing Algorithms\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    oidc:\n      - name: custom-provider\n        issuer_url: \"https://custom.example.com\"\n        algorithms: [\"RS256\", \"ES256\", \"HS256\"]  # NEW: support multiple algorithms\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Support OIDC providers that don't use RS256 for ID token signing.\n\n#### Secret References in OIDC Config (v2.5.0)\n```yaml\nauthentication:\n  methods:\n    oidc:\n      - name: okta\n        client_id: \"${secret:file:okta/client_id}\"\n        client_secret: \"${secret:file:okta/client_secret}\"\n```\n\n**Syntax:** `${secret:file:path/to/secret}` or `${secret:env:ENV_VAR_NAME}`\n\n### Configurable Flag Metadata in ListFlags (v2.3.0)\n\n**API:** REST and gRPC ListFlags endpoints\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nserver:\n  api:\n    list_flags:\n      include_metadata: false  # Default: only include when explicitly requested\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Control whether flag metadata is exposed in public ListFlags responses. Useful for hiding internal metadata in public APIs.\n\n**Example Request:**\n```\nGET /api/v1/namespaces/default/flags?include_metadata=true\n```\n\n### Git Fetch Policy Configuration (v2.3.0)\n\n**API:** Storage Backend Configuration\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  default:\n    fetch_policy: \"lenient\"  # or \"strict\" (default)\n```\n\n**Options:**\n- `strict` (default): Fail startup if remote fetch fails\n- `lenient`: Continue with stale local data if fetch fails\n\n**Use Case:** Enable offline/degraded mode for resilience when Git remote is temporarily unavailable.\n\n### Custom Commit and PR Templates (v2.5.0)\n\n**API:** Storage Configuration\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\nstorage:\n  default:\n    templates:\n      commit_message: \"[flipt] {{.Resource}} {{.Action}}\\n\\nAutomated change by {{.Author}}\"\n      proposal_title: \"Flipt: Update features on {{.Base.Ref}}\"\n      proposal_body: \"Automated proposal\\n\\n- Branch: {{.Branch.Ref}}\\n- Base: {{.Base.Ref}}\"\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Customize commit messages and pull request titles/bodies for Git integration.\n\n### Boolean Evaluation Enhanced (v2.2.0)\n\n**API:** Evaluation Service\n**New Response Field:** Boolean evaluation responses now include matched `segment_keys`\n\n**Example:**\n```json\n{\n  \"enabled\": true,\n  \"reason\": \"MATCH_EVALUATION_REASON\",\n  \"segment_keys\": [\"segment_1\", \"segment_2\"],\n  \"flag_key\": \"my_flag\",\n  \"timestamp\": \"2026-02-17T00:00:00Z\"\n}\n```\n\n**Benefit:** Provides visibility into which segments matched, improving debuggability.\n\n### Streaming Evaluation (v2.1.1+)\n\n**API:** ClientEvaluationService\n**Endpoint:**\n```\nGET /client/v2/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{key}/stream\n```\n\n**Message Types:**\n```protobuf\nrpc EvaluationSnapshotNamespaceStream(EvaluationNamespaceSnapshotStreamRequest)\n  returns (stream EvaluationNamespaceSnapshot)\n```\n\n**Use Case:** Real-time evaluation data streaming for dashboard updates or client-side caching.\n\n---\n\n## Deprecations\n\n### v1 API Endpoints (Deprecated since v2.0.0)\n\n**Endpoints Affected:**\n- `GET /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags`\n- `GET /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags/{flag_key}`\n- `POST /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_key}/flags`\n- And other `/api/v1/*` endpoints\n\n**Replacement:** Use v2 Environments and Resources APIs:\n```\nGET /api/v2/environments/{environment_key}/namespaces/{namespace_key}/resources/flipt.core.Flag\n```\n\n**Timeline:** Removal planned ~1 year after v2.0.0 (August 2025 \u2192 August 2026)\n\n### Database-Backed Storage (Deprecated since v2.0.0)\n\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\n# DEPRECATED - do not use\nstorage:\n  type: postgres\n  connection_string: \"...\"\n```\n\n**Replacement:** Git-based storage is now the standard\n```yaml\n# Use this instead\nstorage:\n  default:\n    remote: \"...\"\n    backend:\n      type: \"memory\"\n```\n\n**Timeline:** Complete removal planned ~1 year after v2.0.0\n\n### Session Token Offset Parameter (Deprecated in v2.0+)\n\n**API:** ListFlagRequest\n**Deprecated Field:**\n```protobuf\nmessage ListFlagRequest {\n  int32 limit = 1;\n  int32 offset = 2 [deprecated = true];  // DEPRECATED: use page_token instead\n  string page_token = 3;  // USE THIS\n  ...\n}\n```\n\n**Migration:**\n```go\n// Before\nGetFlags(ctx, &flipt.ListFlagRequest{\n  Offset: 0,\n  Limit: 10,\n})\n\n// After\nGetFlags(ctx, &flipt.ListFlagRequest{\n  Limit: 10,\n  PageToken: \"\", // empty string for first page\n})\n```\n\n### OpenTelemetry gRPC Interceptors (Deprecated in v2.4.0)\n\n**Configuration:**\n```yaml\n# DEPRECATED gRPC interceptor style\nserver:\n  grpc:\n    interceptors:\n      - otel\n```\n\n**Replacement:** Stats handler approach (automatically used in v2.4.0+)\n```go\n// Modern approach - automatically configured\n// Use stats handler for complete tracing coverage\n```\n\n---\n\n## Bug Fixes\n\n### Critical Fixes\n\n#### Segment Deletion Validation (v2.3.0)\n- **Issue:** Segments could be deleted even when referenced by rules or rollouts\n- **Fix:** Added validation to prevent deletion of segments with active references\n- **Impact:** Database integrity protection\n\n#### Streaming Evaluation HTTP/2 Support (v2.1.1)\n- **Issue:** Streaming evaluation only worked over gRPC, not HTTP/2\n- **Fix:** Accept HTTP/2 connections for streaming evaluation endpoints\n- **Impact:** Broader client compatibility\n\n#### Environment Context Handling (v2.1.1)\n- **Issue:** Error not returned when environment not found in context\n- **Fix:** Properly return error from `GetFromContext` when environment missing\n- **Impact:** Better error diagnostics\n\n### Important Fixes\n\n#### Git Remote Synchronization (v2.4.0)\n- **Issue:** Git remote URLs could become stale if configuration changed\n- **Fix:** Auto-sync remote URLs when configuration is updated\n- **Impact:** Prevents sync failures after config changes\n\n#### Git Connection Error Handling (v2.4.0)\n- **Issue:** DNS resolution and I/O timeout errors not properly detected\n- **Fix:** Properly handle connection errors to allow lenient fetch policy to work\n- **Impact:** Better offline mode support\n\n#### Git Ref Update After Fetch (v2.6.0)\n- **Issue:** Shallow fetches didn't persist references to `refs/heads/`\n- **Fix:** Complete ref update for both bare and normal repositories\n- **Impact:** Proper branch tracking in Git operations\n\n#### Evaluation Environment Lookup (v2.3.1)\n- **Issue:** Duplicate environment retrieval logic with inconsistent fallback behavior\n- **Fix:** Extracted reusable helper method for consistent lookup\n- **Impact:** Reduced code duplication and bugs\n\n#### License Key Format Handling (v2.6.0)\n- **Issue:** License activation wizard failed with annual license key format\n- **Fix:** Support both monthly and annual license key formats\n- **Impact:** Improved Pro license activation UX\n\n#### Redis Configuration Schema (v2.3.0)\n- **Issue:** Redis mode configuration accepted empty string\n- **Fix:** Set default Redis mode to \"single\" instead of empty string\n- **Impact:** More explicit configuration validation\n\n#### Form Submission UX (v2.3.0, v2.3.1)\n- **Issue:** Enter key in tag input submitted entire form unexpectedly\n- **Fix:** Properly handle Enter key for tag addition vs form submission\n- **Impact:** Better UI form handling\n\n### Analytics Fixes\n\n#### Batch Analytics Processing (v2.1.3)\n- **Issue:** Batch analytics returned partial data for requested flags\n- **Fix:** Return all batch data for requested flags\n- **Impact:** Complete analytics visibility\n\n#### Analytics Metadata Events (v2.3.0)\n- **Issue:** Batch evaluation endpoint missing OpenTelemetry tracking\n- **Fix:** Add event tracking to batch evaluation for observability\n- **Impact:** Complete tracing of batch operations\n\n---\n\n## Upgrade Guide\n\n### General Upgrade Process\n\n1. **Backup Configuration and Data**\n   ```bash\n   # Export current flags if upgrading from v1\n   flipt export --format=json > flags_backup.json\n\n   # Backup Git repository\n   git clone --mirror https://your-repo.git flipt-backup.git.mirror\n   ```\n\n2. **Update Flipt Binary**\n   ```bash\n   # Using official releases\n   curl -fsSL https://install.flipt.io | bash\n\n   # Or using container\n   docker pull flipt/flipt:v2.7.0\n   ```\n\n3. **Update Configuration File**\n   Review `/etc/flipt/config.yml` (or your config location) for required changes:\n   - Storage configuration format\n   - Authentication method configurations\n   - Any deprecated options\n\n4. **Verify Environment Variables**\n   Check all `FLIPT_*` environment variables are compatible with new version\n\n5. **Start Flipt**\n   ```bash\n   systemctl restart flipt\n   # or\n   docker-compose up -d\n   ```\n\n6. **Verify Endpoints**\n   Test core endpoints:\n   ```bash\n   # Health check\n default:\n    remote: \"https://github.com/your-org/flipt-features.git\"\n    branch: \"main\"\n    backend:\n      type: \"local\"\n      path: \"/var/lib/flipt/storage\"\n    credentials:\n      type: \"github\"\n      token: \"${secret:file:/etc/flipt/github_token}\"\n\nenvironments:\n  default:\n    storage: \"default\"\n```\n\n**Step 3: Migrate Flags (if applicable)**\n```bash\n# Option A: Export from v1, import to v2\nflipt export --format=json > /tmp/flags.json\nflipt import --format=json < /tmp/flags.json\n\n# Option B: Manually recreate flags via v2 API\n# See Section \"New Features\" for v2 API examples\n```\n\n**Step 4: Update Client SDKs**\n```go\n// Before (v1)\nclient := flipt.NewClient(\n    flipt.WithAddress(\"localhost:8080\"),\n)\nresult, _ := client.Evaluation.Boolean(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    NamespaceKey: \"default\",\n    FlagKey: \"my_flag\",\n    EntityId: \"user-123\",\n    Context: map[string]string{},\n})\n\n// After (v2)\nclient := flipt.NewClient(\n    flipt.WithAddress(\"localhost:8080\"),\n)\nresult, _ := client.Evaluation.Boolean(ctx, &flipt.EvaluationRequest{\n    EnvironmentKey: \"production\",  // NEW: required\n    NamespaceKey: \"default\",\n    FlagKey: \"my_flag\",\n    EntityId: \"user-123\",\n    Context: map[string]string{},\n})\n```\n\n### Upgrading from v2.x to v2.y\n\nThese are minor/patch upgrades with good backwards compatibility:\n\n**For v2.5.0 \u2192 v2.6.0:**\n- GitHub App auth is now available as an alternative to PAT\n- OIDC configuration enhancements are optional\n- No breaking changes; upgrade and redeploy\n\n**For v2.6.0 \u2192 v2.7.0:**\n- Go 1.26 and go-git v6 dependencies updated\n- SigV4 auth for Prometheus is optional\n- Default Git commit email updated (more appropriate value)\n- No breaking changes; standard upgrade\n\n**For any v2.x upgrade:**\n```bash\n# 1. Pull latest version\ndocker pull flipt/flipt:v2.7.0\n\n# 2. Verify configuration compatibility\nflipt validate-config --config=/etc/flipt/config.yml\n\n# 3. Restart Flipt\nsystemctl restart flipt\n# or\ndocker-compose up -d --force-recreate\n\n# 4. Check logs for warnings/errors\njournalctl -u flipt -f\n# or\ndocker-compose logs -f flipt\n```\n\n### Configuration Validation\n\nFlipt provides a validation command:\n```bash\n# Validate configuration before deploying\nflipt validate-config --config=./config.yml\n\n# With verbose output\nflipt validate-config --config=./config.yml --verbose\n```\n\n### Monitoring the Upgrade\n\nKey metrics to monitor:\n\n1. **API Error Rate**\n   ```promql\n   rate(flipt_server_request_duration_count{status=\"error\"}[5m])\n   ```\n\n2. **Evaluation Latency**\n   ```promql\n   histogram_quantile(0.95,\n     rate(flipt_evaluation_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])\n   )\n   ```\n\n3. **Git Sync Status**\n   ```promql\n   flipt_git_sync_duration_seconds_bucket\n   flipt_git_sync_errors_total\n   ```\n\n### Rollback Procedures\n\n**For Docker Deployments:**\n```bash\n# Quickly rollback to previous version\ndocker-compose down\ndocker-compose.yml  # Restore previous version\ndocker-compose up -d\n```\n\n**For Systemd Deployments:**\n```bash\nsystemctl stop flipt\n# Restore previous binary version\n/usr/local/bin/flipt  # downgrade\nsystemctl start flipt\n```\n\n**For Kubernetes Deployments:**\n```bash\n# Rollback to previous deployment\nkubectl rollout undo deployment/flipt\nkubectl rollout status deployment/flipt\n```\n\n### Common Troubleshooting\n\n**Issue: 404 errors on v1 API endpoints**\n- **Cause:** v1 endpoints are still available but require explicit migration\n- **Solution:** Update client SDKs to use v2 APIs as documented in \"Breaking Changes\"\n\n**Issue: Git authentication failures after upgrade**\n- **Cause:** Credentials format may have changed\n- **Solution:** Verify Git credentials in configuration using secret references\n\n**Issue: Evaluation requests return \"environment not found\"**\n- **Cause:** `environment_key` parameter now required (v2.3.0+)\n- **Solution:** Update evaluation requests to include explicit `environment_key` field\n\n**Issue: High memory usage after upgrade**\n- **Cause:** OpenTelemetry or ClickHouse integration in v2.1.3+ requires tuning\n- **Solution:** Review analytics storage configuration and batch buffer settings\n\n---\n\n## Summary Table\n\n| Feature | Introduced | Status | Migration Required |\n|---------|------------|--------|-------------------|\n| # Flipt Release Notes

Comprehensive summary of API changes in recent Flipt releases. Flipt is a Git-native feature flag management system with REST and gRPC APIs for managing feature flags, segments, and environments.

## Table of Contents

- [Breaking Changes](#breaking-changes)
- [New Features](#new-features)
- [Deprecations](#deprecations)
- [Bug Fixes](#bug-fixes)
- [Upgrade Guide](#upgrade-guide)

---

## Breaking Changes

These changes require action from users upgrading.

### Configuration Schema Changes (v2.0+)

**Affected API:** Storage Configuration
**Since:** v2.0.0

The storage configuration format has fundamentally changed to support Git-native operations:

**Before (v1.x):**
```yaml
# Database-backed storage
storage:
  type: postgres
  connection_string: "..."
```

**After (v2.0+):**
```yaml
# Git-based storage
storage:
  default:
    remote: "https://github.com/user/flags.git"
    branch: "main"
    backend:
      type: "memory"  # or "local"
    credentials:
      type: "github"
      token: "..."
```

**Migration Path:**
1. Migrating from v1 Flipt requires exporting all flags and segments from the old database
2. Create a new Git repository for storing feature flag definitions
3. Initialize Flipt with Git storage configuration pointing to the new repository
4. Import previously exported flags via the v2 API
5. Refer to [Git Storage Configuration Documentation](https://docs.flipt.io/latest/configuration/storage) for detailed steps

### REST API v1 Endpoint Changes

**Affected API:** `/api/v1/*` endpoints
**Status:** Deprecated (still available but not recommended)

While v1 endpoints are preserved for backwards compatibility, they are no longer the primary API surface. Migrate to v2 APIs:

**v1 ListFlags Example:**
```
GET /api/v1/namespaces/{namespace_
... (truncated)
